I think the amenities are very nice and clean but are an extra charge to use and have some restrictive rules, such as being required to wear a swim cap in the pool. I think this hotel is more for business travelers, the rooms offer great work space and the hotel offers great meeting spaces.

msg:Breakfast is rich and great!
The dining environment is very good!

I have almost never photographed restaurants^the corpse of food^, and even food is just a necessity for me to survive.
But if Chinese food elements can be added to Chinese restaurants, it will make people‚Äôs eyes brighten and come back again and again!
This is rice roll, as big as a ********* egg pancake. Add a little salt and soy sauce to enhance the flavor, it tastes good.
Disadvantages: The pastry is too thick and the fillings are too little. If the shrimps are thin-skinned, it will remind me of Hong Kong-style rice rolls.

I ate 3 bowls of raw porridge. The first bowl is preserved egg and lean meat porridge, and the second bowl is beef porridge. Eat freshly cooked porridge for breakfast, which warms my Oriental stomach. Very tasty!
The disadvantage is: this is really porridge. Whether it is preserved eggs, lean meat or beef, you have to use a magnifying glass to look for it in the porridge.
For the third bowl, I asked the freshly cooked chef to cook another bowl of beef porridge, but the amount of beef must be tripled.
This time, it‚Äôs really the beef porridge I want.

msg:Because I bought a ticket for the Youth Olympics concert at short notice, I chose Hualuxe Hotel because it was close to the Youth Olympics Pavilion. I read the reviews of several guests, and the actual experience and stay experience were even more positive.
First of all, it is very suitable for watching concerts. It is just across the Rainbow Bridge from the venue. For those with fast feet like me, it takes less than 4 minutes to get from the hotel to the stadium. (The hotel will open the Rainbow Bridge within a certain time period after receiving the notice of the performance.) There is no need to worry about the journey back to the hotel after the performance. After watching the show, I went back to the hotel to take a bath and sleep. It was very convenient and safe.
Secondly, I was very lucky that Manager Li received me during check-in. He is very considerate and provides convenience for the guests. He is considerate, clear in thinking, kind and courteous, and makes people feel very comfortable. He makes the guests feel at home on the front line. During my stay, I met him every day to say hello. After checking out, I waited for him to say goodbye and thanked him for taking care of me during this period.
Again, the two-bedroom suite is really suitable for families. The room is large, spacious, clean, and has a good view. You can see the two Youth Olympic venues and the Rainbow Bridge outside the window, and the small football field on the other side. The bathroom facilities are complete and the hardware has reached five-star standards.
Finally, let‚Äôs talk about catering. Because of the executive trea**ent, all three meals and afternoon tea are in the hotel. The breakfast was indeed as everyone reported, very rich, with a wide range of choices and Cantonese characteristics. Afternoon tea is at the lobby bar, dinner is at Eheng, until 8 pm. I go to see a show or go out for fun, and my elderly family members stay in the hotel to enjoy food and rest, which is very reassuring.
All in all, I made a wise choice this time and had a great experience. I would recommend it to everyone.

1. One week before traveling, call to inquire and confirm your room type preference, whether it is a double bed or a twin bed, and make a note
